\doxysubsection{详细描述}
\subsubsection*{template$<$class RCU, typename Key, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$\newline
class cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Ellen\+Bin\+Tree$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}
Ellen\textquotesingle{}s et al binary search tree (RCU specialization) 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu}%
 Source\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item \mbox{[}2010\mbox{]} F.\+Ellen, P.\+Fatourou, E.\+Ruppert, F.\+van Breugel "{}\+Non-\/blocking Binary Search Tree"{}
\end{DoxyItemize}

Ellen\+Bin\+Tree is an unbalanced leaf-\/oriented binary search tree that implements the {\itshape set} abstract data type. Nodes maintains child pointers but not parent pointers. Every internal node has exactly two children, and all data of type {\ttfamily T} currently in the tree are stored in the leaves. Internal nodes of the tree are used to direct {\ttfamily find} operation along the path to the correct leaf. The keys (of {\ttfamily Key} type) stored in internal nodes may or may not be in the set. {\ttfamily Key} type is a subset of {\ttfamily T} type. There should be exactly defined a key extracting functor for converting object of type {\ttfamily T} to object of type {\ttfamily Key}.

Due to {\ttfamily extract\+\_\+min} and {\ttfamily extract\+\_\+max} member functions the {\ttfamily Ellen\+Bin\+Tree} can act as a {\itshape priority queue}. In this case you should provide unique compound key, for example, the priority value plus some uniformly distributed random value.

\begin{DoxyAttention}{注意}
Recall the tree is {\bfseries{unbalanced}}. The complexity of operations is {\ttfamily O(log N)} for uniformly distributed random keys, but in the worst case the complexity is {\ttfamily O(\+N)}.
\end{DoxyAttention}
\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
In the current implementation we do not use helping technique described in the original paper. Instead of helping, when a thread encounters a concurrent operation it just spins waiting for the operation done. Such solution allows greatly simplify the implementation of tree.
\end{DoxyNote}
{\bfseries{Template arguments}}\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily RCU} -\/ one of \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type}
\item {\ttfamily Key} -\/ key type, a subset of {\ttfamily T} 
\item {\ttfamily T} -\/ type to be stored in tree\textquotesingle{}s leaf nodes. The type must be based on {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1ellen__bintree_1_1node}{ellen\+\_\+bintree\+::node}} (for {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1ellen__bintree_1_1base__hook}{ellen\+\_\+bintree\+::base\+\_\+hook}}) or it must have a member of type {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1ellen__bintree_1_1node}{ellen\+\_\+bintree\+::node}} (for {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1ellen__bintree_1_1member__hook}{ellen\+\_\+bintree\+::member\+\_\+hook}}).
\item {\ttfamily Traits} -\/ tree traits, default is {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1ellen__bintree_1_1traits}{ellen\+\_\+bintree\+::traits}} It is possible to declare option-\/based tree with {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1ellen__bintree_1_1make__traits}{ellen\+\_\+bintree\+::make\+\_\+traits}} metafunction instead of {\ttfamily Traits} template argument.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Before including {\ttfamily \texorpdfstring{$<$}{<}\doxylink{ellen__bintree__rcu_8h}{cds/intrusive/ellen\+\_\+bintree\+\_\+rcu.\+h}\texorpdfstring{$>$}{>}} you should include appropriate RCU header file, see \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1urcu_cds_urcu_gc}{RCU type} for list of existing RCU class and corresponding header files.
\end{DoxyNote}
\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_less}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_less}%
{\bfseries{Predicate requirements}}

{\ttfamily Traits\+::less}, {\ttfamily Traits\+::compare} and other predicates using with member fuctions should accept at least parameters of type {\ttfamily T} and {\ttfamily Key} in any combination. For example, for {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_foo}{Foo}} struct with {\ttfamily std\+::string} key field the appropiate {\ttfamily less} functor is\+:

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_usage}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_usage}%
{\bfseries{Usage}}

Suppose we have the following \doxylink{struct_foo}{Foo} struct with string key type\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{Foo}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{std::string}}\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{m\_strKey}}\ \ \ \ ;\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ key}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//...\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ other\ non-\/key\ data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


We want to utilize RCU-\/based {\ttfamily cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Ellen\+Bin\+Tree} set for {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_foo}{Foo}} data. We may use base hook or member hook. Consider base hook variant. First, we need deriving {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_foo}{Foo}} struct from {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1ellen__bintree_1_1node}{cds\+::intrusive\+::ellen\+\_\+bintree\+::node}}\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{preprocessor}{\#include\ <\mbox{\hyperlink{general__buffered_8h}{cds/urcu/general\_buffered.h}}>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{preprocessor}{\#include\ <\mbox{\hyperlink{ellen__bintree__rcu_8h}{cds/intrusive/ellen\_bintree\_rcu.h}}>}}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ RCU\ type\ we\ use}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{typedef}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{cds::urcu::gc<\ cds::urcu::general\_buffered<>}}\ >\ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{gpb\_rcu}};}
\DoxyCodeLine{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{Foo}}:\ \textcolor{keyword}{public}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{cds::intrusive}}:\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{ellen\_bintree::node}}<\ gpb\_rcu\ >}
\DoxyCodeLine{\{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{std::string}}\ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{m\_strKey}}\ \ \ \ ;\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ The\ key}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//...\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ other\ non-\/key\ data}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


Second, we need to implement auxiliary structures and functors\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item key extractor functor for extracting the key from {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_foo}{Foo}} object. Such functor is necessary because the tree internal nodes store the keys.
\item {\ttfamily less} predicate. We want our set should accept {\ttfamily std\+::string} and {\ttfamily char const \texorpdfstring{$\ast$}{*}} parameters for searching, so our {\ttfamily less} predicate will not be trivial, see below.
\item item counting feature\+: we want our set\textquotesingle{}s {\ttfamily \doxylink{imgui__impl__opengl3__loader_8h_ac42c05b5701aef6bab82675cf3b55fee}{size()}} member function returns actual item count.
\end{DoxyItemize}

\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{comment}{//\ ...}}

\end{DoxyCode}


Instead of declaring {\ttfamily set\+\_\+traits} type traits we can use option-\/based syntax with {\ttfamily \doxylink{structcds_1_1intrusive_1_1ellen__bintree_1_1make__traits}{ellen\+\_\+bintree\+::make\+\_\+traits}} metafunction, for example\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ ,\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{cds::intrusive::ellen\_bintree::key\_extractor<\ my\_key\_extractor\ >}}}

\DoxyCodeLine{>\ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{set\_type2}};}

\end{DoxyCode}


Functionally, {\ttfamily set\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily set\+\_\+type2} are equivalent.

{\bfseries{Member-\/hooked tree}}

Sometimes, we cannot use base hook, for example, when the {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_foo}{Foo}} structure is external. In such case we can use member hook feature.

{\bfseries{Multiple containers}}

Sometimes we need that our {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_foo}{Foo}} struct should be used in several different containers. Suppose, {\ttfamily \doxylink{struct_foo}{Foo}} struct has two key fields\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{Foo}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{std::string}}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{m\_strKey}}\ \ \ \ ;\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ string\ key}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{int}\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{m\_nKey}}\ \ \ \ \ \ ;\ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//\ int\ key}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{comment}{//...\ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ \ //\ other\ non-\/key\ data\ fields}}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


We want to build two intrusive {\ttfamily Ellen\+Bin\+Tree} sets\+: one indexed on {\ttfamily Foo\+::m\+\_\+str\+Key} field, another indexed on {\ttfamily Foo\+::m\+\_\+n\+Key} field. To decide such case we should use a tag option for tree\textquotesingle{}s hook\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{preprocessor}{\#include\ <\mbox{\hyperlink{general__buffered_8h}{cds/urcu/general\_buffered.h}}>}}

Clears the tree (thread safe, not atomic) 

The function unlink all items from the tree. The function is thread safe but not atomic\+: in multi-\/threaded environment with parallel insertions this sequence 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{set}}.\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a5c0fe86f1ae1ff30607eecd18f64e258}{clear}}();}

\end{DoxyCode}
 the assertion could be raised.

For each leaf the \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a5f14b96ac47e63feab582d27c857fe2c}{disposer} will be called after unlinking.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked. 函数调用图\+:

Checks whether the set contains {\ttfamily key} 

The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns {\ttfamily true} if it is found, and {\ttfamily false} otherwise.

The function applies RCU lock internally. 函数调用图\+:

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Ellen\+Bin\+Tree}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::contains (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Checks whether the set contains {\ttfamily key} using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is similar to {\ttfamily contains( key )} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less} and should meet \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_less}{Predicate requirements}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. {\ttfamily pred} should accept arguments of type {\ttfamily Q}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_af5c6b62e5002f389473533d0d8e185da}{key\+\_\+type}}, {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_add56a738dd647d7d4afee42ba853cd49}{value\+\_\+type}} in any combination. 函数调用图\+:

Checks whether the set contains {\ttfamily key} using {\ttfamily pred} predicate for searching 

The function is similar to {\ttfamily contains( key )} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less}. {\ttfamily Less} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the set. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ab133b5a334a91ce6698c9efedf483c8d}\index{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!empty@{empty}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Ellen\+Bin\+Tree}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::erase (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&}]{key}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Deletes the item from the tree 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_erase}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_erase}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the tree, unlinks it from the tree, and returns {\ttfamily true}. If the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} is not found the function return {\ttfamily false}.

Note the {\ttfamily Traits\+::less} and/or {\ttfamily Traits\+::compare} predicate should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_add56a738dd647d7d4afee42ba853cd49}{value\+\_\+type}}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a22171203a1350b378388367be87f1705}\index{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!erase@{erase}}

Deletes the item from the tree 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_erase_func}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_erase_func}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the tree, call {\ttfamily f} functor with item found, unlinks it from the tree, and returns {\ttfamily true}. The \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a5f14b96ac47e63feab582d27c857fe2c}{disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} class template parameter is called by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} asynchronously.

The {\ttfamily Func} interface is 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{functor}}\ \{}

\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}


If the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} is not found the function return {\ttfamily false}.

Note the {\ttfamily Traits\+::less} and/or {\ttfamily Traits\+::compare} predicate should accept a parameter of type {\ttfamily Q} that can be not the same as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_add56a738dd647d7d4afee42ba853cd49}{value\+\_\+type}}.

Delete the item from the tree with comparing functor {\ttfamily pred} 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_erase}{erase(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} predicate is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less} and should meet \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_less}{Predicate requirements}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the tree. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a51012c5184cc2c06f66ee432a3fc9f07}\index{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!erase\_with@{erase\_with}}

Delete the item from the tree with comparing functor {\ttfamily pred} 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_erase_func}{erase(Q const\&, Func)} but {\ttfamily pred} predicate is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less} and should meet \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_less}{Predicate requirements}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the tree. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a7db71821513ed5c506a309d86a0fac4d}\index{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!extract@{extract}}

template$<$class RCU, typename Key, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\

Extracts an item from the tree 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_extract}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_extract}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the tree, unlinks it, and returns \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1exempt__ptr}{exempt\+\_\+ptr} pointer to an item found. If the item with the key equal to {\ttfamily key} is not found the function returns empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_afcb733ae1e60a5beb86fd902c0a38071}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}}.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should NOT be locked. The function does not call the disposer for the item found. The disposer will be implicitly invoked when the returned object is destroyed or when its {\ttfamily release()} member function is called. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a5ecfd262bfa423fa5d2060455cffd765}\index{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!extract@{extract}}
\index{extract@{extract}!cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract()}{extract()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}

Extracts an item from the tree 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_extract}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_extract}%
The function searches an item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} in the tree, unlinks it, and returns a guarded pointer to an item found. If the item is not found the function returns an empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a007f95a47cac63b2c14cd25d5cfb50d8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}}.

{\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a007f95a47cac63b2c14cd25d5cfb50d8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} prevents disposer invocation for returned item, see cds\+::gc\+::guarded\+\_\+ptr for explanation. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a007f95a47cac63b2c14cd25d5cfb50d8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource. 
\end{DoxyNote}

Extracts an item with maximal key from the tree 

The function searches an item with maximal key, unlinks it, and returns \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1exempt__ptr}{exempt\+\_\+ptr} pointer to the rightmost item. If the tree is empty the function returns empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_afcb733ae1e60a5beb86fd902c0a38071}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Due the concurrent nature of the tree, the function extracts {\itshape nearly} maximal key. It means that the function gets rightmost leaf of the tree and tries to unlink it. During unlinking, a concurrent thread may insert an item with key great than rightmost item\textquotesingle{}s key. So, the function returns the item with maximum key at the moment of tree traversing.
\end{DoxyNote}
RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should NOT be locked. The function does not call the disposer for the item found. The disposer will be implicitly invoked when the returned object is destroyed or when its {\ttfamily release()} member function is called. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a66fef3313f95b887854de03dd7032140}\index{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!extract\_max@{extract\_max}}
\index{extract\_max@{extract\_max}!cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract\_max()}{extract\_max()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a66fef3313f95b887854de03dd7032140} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a007f95a47cac63b2c14cd25d5cfb50d8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Ellen\+Bin\+Tree}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+max (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item with maximal key from the tree 

The function searches an item with maximal key, unlinks it, and returns a guarded pointer to an item found. If the tree is empty the function returns an empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a007f95a47cac63b2c14cd25d5cfb50d8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Due the concurrent nature of the tree, the function extracts {\itshape nearly} maximal key. It means that the function gets rightmost leaf of the tree and tries to unlink it. During unlinking, a concurrent thread may insert an item with key great than rightmost item\textquotesingle{}s key. So, the function returns the item with maximal key at the moment of tree traversing.
\end{DoxyNote}
The returned {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a007f95a47cac63b2c14cd25d5cfb50d8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} prevents disposer invocation for returned item, see cds\+::gc\+::guarded\+\_\+ptr for explanation. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a007f95a47cac63b2c14cd25d5cfb50d8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource. 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a524390f3d77ca7f58b13dcd3f751c7c8} 
template$<$class RCU, typename Key, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_afcb733ae1e60a5beb86fd902c0a38071}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Ellen\+Bin\+Tree}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+min (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item with minimal key from the tree 

The function searches an item with minimal key, unlinks it, and returns \doxylink{classcds_1_1urcu_1_1exempt__ptr}{exempt\+\_\+ptr} pointer to the leftmost item. If the tree is empty the function returns empty {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_afcb733ae1e60a5beb86fd902c0a38071}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}}.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Due the concurrent nature of the tree, the function extracts {\itshape nearly} minimum key. It means that the function gets leftmost leaf of the tree and tries to unlink it. During unlinking, a concurrent thread may insert an item with key less than leftmost item\textquotesingle{}s key. So, the function returns the item with minimum key at the moment of tree traversing.
\end{DoxyNote}
RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should NOT be locked. The function does not call the disposer for the item found. The disposer will be implicitly invoked when the returned object is destroyed or when its {\ttfamily release()} member function is called. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a7b4b540395597d0a296ef01fd15568f3}\index{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!extract\_min@{extract\_min}}
\index{extract\_min@{extract\_min}!cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a007f95a47cac63b2c14cd25d5cfb50d8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Ellen\+Bin\+Tree}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+min (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item with minimal key from the tree 

The function searches an item with minimal key, unlinks it, and returns a guarded pointer to an item found. If the tree is empty the function returns an empty guarded pointer.

\begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Due the concurrent nature of the tree, the function extracts {\itshape nearly} minimum key. It means that the function gets leftmost leaf of the tree and tries to unlink it. During unlinking, a concurrent thread may insert an item with key less than leftmost item\textquotesingle{}s key. So, the function returns the item with minimum key at the moment of tree traversing.
\end{DoxyNote}
The returned {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a007f95a47cac63b2c14cd25d5cfb50d8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} prevents disposer invocation for returned item, see {\ttfamily cds\+::gc\+::guarded\+\_\+ptr} for explanation. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a007f95a47cac63b2c14cd25d5cfb50d8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource. 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a582d238f8eb62f6a58d3faa75f85a972}

template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Less$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_afcb733ae1e60a5beb86fd902c0a38071}{exempt\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Ellen\+Bin\+Tree}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::extract\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Extracts an item from the set using {\ttfamily pred} for searching 

The function is an analog of {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a7db71821513ed5c506a309d86a0fac4d}{extract(\+Q const\&)}} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key compare. {\ttfamily Less} has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less} and should meet \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_less}{predicate requirements}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the tree. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_af9bc89890f38d35520dc3572efc35a2e}\index{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!extract\_with@{extract\_with}}
\index{extract\_with@{extract\_with}!cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{extract\_with()}{extract\_with()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_af9bc89890f38d35520dc3572efc35a2e}

Extracts an item from the tree using {\ttfamily pred} for searching 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_extract}{extract(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key compare. {\ttfamily Less} has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less} and should meet \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_less}{Predicate requirements}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the tree. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ae5bc2ce2bbf87fe3ba6599125d02e113}\index{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!find@{find}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ae5bc2ce2bbf87fe3ba6599125d02e113} 
template$<$class RCU, typename Key, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}}, typename Func$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Ellen\+Bin\+Tree}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::find (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds the key {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_find_func}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_find_func}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and calls the functor {\ttfamily f} for item found. The interface of {\ttfamily Func} functor is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keyword}{struct\ }\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{functor}}\ \{}
\DoxyCodeLine{\ \ \ \ \textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{operator()}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{Q}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{key}}\ );}
\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily item} is the item found, {\ttfamily key} is the {\ttfamily find} function argument.

The functor can change non-\/key fields of {\ttfamily item}. Note that the functor is only guarantee that {\ttfamily item} cannot be disposed during functor is executing. The functor does not serialize simultaneous access to the tree {\ttfamily item}. If such access is possible you must provide your own synchronization schema on item level to exclude unsafe item modifications.

The function applies RCU lock internally.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily key} is found, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. 函数调用图\+:

Finds the key {\ttfamily key} 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_find_func}%

\begin{DoxyCode}{0}

\DoxyCodeLine{\};}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily item} is the item found, {\ttfamily key} is the {\ttfamily find} function argument.

The functor can change non-\/key fields of {\ttfamily item}. Note that the functor is only guarantee that {\ttfamily item} cannot be disposed during functor is executing. The functor does not serialize simultaneous access to the tree {\ttfamily item}. If such access is possible you must provide your own synchronization schema on item level to exclude unsafe item modifications.

Finds the key {\ttfamily key} with comparing functor {\ttfamily pred} 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_find_func}{find(Q\&, Func)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparison. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less} and should meet \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_less}{Predicate requirements}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the tree. 函数调用图\+:

Finds {\ttfamily key} and return the item found 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_get}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_get}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns the pointer to item found. If {\ttfamily key} is not found it returns {\ttfamily nullptr}.

RCU should be locked before call the function. Returned pointer is valid while RCU is locked. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_afa3db45989ed4a47acc07e00b8457e5a}\index{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!get@{get}}

Finds {\ttfamily key} and returns the item found 

\label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_get}%
\Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_get}%
The function searches the item with key equal to {\ttfamily key} and returns the item found as {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a007f95a47cac63b2c14cd25d5cfb50d8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object. The function returns an empty guarded pointer is {\ttfamily key} is not found.

{\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a007f95a47cac63b2c14cd25d5cfb50d8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} prevents disposer invocation for returned item, see {\ttfamily cds\+::gc\+::guarded\+\_\+ptr} for explanation. \begin{DoxyNote}{注解}
Each {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a007f95a47cac63b2c14cd25d5cfb50d8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} object uses the GC\textquotesingle{}s guard that can be limited resource. 
\end{DoxyNote}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ac0bd93c32453804fe0ca4e8c8c11525c}

Finds {\ttfamily key} with {\ttfamily pred} predicate and return the item found 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_rcu_get}{get(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for comparing the keys.

{\ttfamily Less} functor has the semantics like {\ttfamily std\+::less} but should take arguments of type \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_add56a738dd647d7d4afee42ba853cd49}{value\+\_\+type} and {\ttfamily Q} in any order. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the tree. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a65ef19bb11bb7dd9f624b2233d35f79c}\index{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!get\_with@{get\_with}}
\index{get\_with@{get\_with}!cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{get\_with()}{get\_with()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a65ef19bb11bb7dd9f624b2233d35f79c} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a007f95a47cac63b2c14cd25d5cfb50d8}{guarded\+\_\+ptr}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Ellen\+Bin\+Tree}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::get\+\_\+with (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{_householder_q_r__householder_q_8cpp_a7e56035a736d269ad670f312496a0846}{Q}} const \&}]{key}{, }\item[{Less}]{pred}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption}) const\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Finds {\ttfamily key} with predicate {\ttfamily pred} and returns the item found 

The function is an analog of \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_get}{get(Q const\&)} but {\ttfamily pred} is used for key comparing. {\ttfamily Less} functor has the interface like {\ttfamily std\+::less} and should meet \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_cds_intrusive_EllenBinTree_less}{Predicate requirements}. {\ttfamily pred} must imply the same element order as the comparator used for building the tree. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a02172bcb0d7173db7c6eae9967a1fa28}\index{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Ellen\+Bin\+Tree}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_add56a738dd647d7d4afee42ba853cd49}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

The function inserts {\ttfamily val} in the tree if it does not contain an item with key equal to {\ttfamily val}.

The function applies RCU lock internally.

Returns {\ttfamily true} if {\ttfamily val} is placed into the set, {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a8c43f98b99ad30b3ac6376e05af049db}\index{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!insert@{insert}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a720938b154f0d19179a7a92610ed459b} 
template$<$class RCU, typename Key, typename \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, class Traits$>$ \\
template$<$typename Func$>$ \\
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Ellen\+Bin\+Tree}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::insert (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_add56a738dd647d7d4afee42ba853cd49}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{f}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Inserts new node 

This function is intended for derived non-\/intrusive containers.

The function allows to split creating of new item into two part\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item create item with key only
\item insert new item into the tree
\item if inserting is success, calls {\ttfamily f} functor to initialize value-\/field of {\ttfamily val}.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_add56a738dd647d7d4afee42ba853cd49}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 where {\ttfamily val} is the item inserted. User-\/defined functor {\ttfamily f} should guarantee that during changing {\ttfamily val} no any other changes could be made on this tree\textquotesingle{}s item by concurrent threads. The user-\/defined functor is called only if the inserting is success.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked. 函数调用图\+:
% FIG 9

Returns item count in the tree 

Only leaf nodes containing user data are counted.

The value returned depends on item counter type provided by {\ttfamily Traits} template parameter. If it is {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1atomicity_1_1empty__item__counter}{atomicity\+::empty\+\_\+item\+\_\+counter}} this function always returns 0.

The function is not suitable for checking the tree emptiness, use {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ab133b5a334a91ce6698c9efedf483c8d}{empty()}} member function for that. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_a58a405d398a2468d54e4cc78f09c6a40}\index{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!size@{size}}

\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Ellen\+Bin\+Tree}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::unlink (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_add56a738dd647d7d4afee42ba853cd49}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Unlinks the item {\ttfamily val} from the tree 

The function searches the item {\ttfamily val} in the tree and unlink it from the tree if it is found and is equal to {\ttfamily val}.

Difference between {\ttfamily \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ab1be3aa2a573ac843f86a45760f9c933}{erase()}} and {\ttfamily unlink}() functions\+: {\ttfamily erase}() finds {\itshape a key} and deletes the item found. {\ttfamily unlink}() finds an item by key and deletes it only if {\ttfamily val} is an item of the tree, i.\+e. the pointer to item found is equal to {\ttfamily  \&val }.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked.

The \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_a5f14b96ac47e63feab582d27c857fe2c}{disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} class template parameter is called by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} asynchronously.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if success and {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_ac2a6c46b4b6d495c45d5a738adaf2807}\index{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!unlink@{unlink}}
\index{unlink@{unlink}!cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{unlink()}{unlink()}\hspace{0.1cm}{\footnotesize\ttfamily [2/2]}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_ac2a6c46b4b6d495c45d5a738adaf2807} 
\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Ellen\+Bin\+Tree}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::unlink (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_add56a738dd647d7d4afee42ba853cd49}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Unlinks the item {\ttfamily val} from the tree 

The function searches the item {\ttfamily val} in the tree and unlink it from the tree if it is found and is equal to {\ttfamily val}.

Difference between \doxylink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_ab1be3aa2a573ac843f86a45760f9c933}{erase} and {\ttfamily unlink} functions\+: {\ttfamily erase} finds {\itshape a key} and deletes the item found. {\ttfamily unlink} finds an item by key and deletes it only if {\ttfamily val} is a node, i.\+e. the pointer to item found is equal to {\ttfamily  \&val }.

The {\ttfamily disposer} specified in {\ttfamily Traits} class template parameter is called by garbage collector {\ttfamily GC} asynchronously.

The function returns {\ttfamily true} if success and {\ttfamily false} otherwise. \Hypertarget{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_aa80973361880b66bddef6576598957b2}\index{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$@{cds::intrusive::EllenBinTree$<$ cds::urcu::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, T, Traits $>$}!unsafe\_clear@{unsafe\_clear}}

{\footnotesize\ttfamily \label{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_afe80203ac4c1f64191e2033ff2b7f5dd}

template$<$typename Func$>$ \\
std\+::pair$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}, \mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}} $>$ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{cds\+::intrusive\+::\+Ellen\+Bin\+Tree}}$<$ cds\+::urcu\+::gc$<$ RCU $>$, Key, \mbox{\hyperlink{_tutorial__sparse__example_8cpp_af639fb96631ba0018f0b2259fc95edfb}{T}}, Traits $>$\+::update (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_add56a738dd647d7d4afee42ba853cd49}{value\+\_\+type}} \&}]{val}{, }\item[{Func}]{func}{, }\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{sugar_8h_abb452686968e48b67397da5f97445f5b}{bool}}}]{b\+Allow\+Insert}{ = {\ttfamily \mbox{\hyperlink{yyjson_8h_a41f9c5fb8b08eb5dc3edce4dcb37fee7}{true}}}}\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [inline]}}



Updates the node 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If the item {\ttfamily val} is not found in the set, then {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the set iff {\ttfamily b\+Allow\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, the functor {\ttfamily func} is called with item found. The functor {\ttfamily func} signature is\+: 
\begin{DoxyCode}{0}
\DoxyCodeLine{\textcolor{keywordtype}{void}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{benchmarks_2async__task_2async__task_8hpp_abce53bb5cc1ee70cdc013fd9b93547eb}{func}}(\ \textcolor{keywordtype}{bool}\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{bNew}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_add56a738dd647d7d4afee42ba853cd49}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{item}},\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree_3_01cds_1_1urcu_1_1gc_3_01_r_c_u_01_4_00_01_key_00_01_t_00_01_traits_01_4_add56a738dd647d7d4afee42ba853cd49}{value\_type}}\&\ \mbox{\hyperlink{classcds_1_1intrusive_1_1_ellen_bin_tree}{val}}\ );}

\end{DoxyCode}
 with arguments\+:
\begin{DoxyItemize}
\item {\ttfamily b\+New} -\/ {\ttfamily true} if the item has been inserted, {\ttfamily false} otherwise
\item {\ttfamily item} -\/ item of the set
\item {\ttfamily val} -\/ argument {\ttfamily val} passed into the {\ttfamily update}() function If new item has been inserted (i.\+e. {\ttfamily b\+New} is {\ttfamily true}) then {\ttfamily item} and {\ttfamily val} arguments refer to the same thing.
\end{DoxyItemize}

The functor can change non-\/key fields of the {\ttfamily item}; however, {\ttfamily func} must guarantee that during changing no any other modifications could be made on this item by concurrent threads.

RCU {\ttfamily synchronize} method can be called. RCU should not be locked.

Returns std\+::pair$<$bool, bool$>$ where {\ttfamily first} is {\ttfamily true} if operation is successful, i.\+e. the node has been inserted or updated, {\ttfamily second} is {\ttfamily true} if new item has been added or {\ttfamily false} if the item with {\ttfamily key} already exists.

\begin{DoxyWarning}{警告}
See \doxylink{namespacecds_1_1intrusive_cds_intrusive_item_creating}{insert item troubleshooting} 
\end{DoxyWarning}

Updates the node 

The operation performs inserting or changing data with lock-\/free manner.

If the item {\ttfamily val} is not found in the set, then {\ttfamily val} is inserted into the set iff {\ttfamily b\+Allow\+Insert} is {\ttfamily true}. Otherwise, the functor {\ttfamily func} is called with item found. The functor {\ttfamily func} signature is\+:
